It should be 11 hours and 40 minutes!\r\n\r\nThe proposed calculator will make it easy to provide different calculations between different indicators, considering the fact that one hour has 60 minutes.\r\nThere is no surprise today in addition and subtraction of hours and minutes.\r\n\r\nUnlike other similar calculators, the user can choose the kind of numbers that will be used for calculations (number, time, speed, distance, cost, fuel, consumption, rate). Please note that the preview in this case doesn’t show the result you will get as it depends on what things are at runtime.\r\n\r\nExample for this case might be, assume that you have three files with names: ‘World.txt’, ‘Hello_World.txt’, and ‘Hello_Neighbor.txt’. You replace the word ‘Hello_’ with an empty string. The result will be ‘World.txt’ (no change), ‘Neighbor.txt’, and something like this: ‘World_ab7680b8-26d3-40f9-ab2f-2c76120a667d.txt’.\r\n\r\nThe way the program works (you might notice this, especially when you are, for example, changing case a large amount number of files), is when it sees an existing file with the same name, it will instead rename to a unique temporary name as said above, then continue with other files (that might or might not include that existing file). Then it comes back working with that unique temporary name, and determine whether to leave as that name currently is, or change to your desired name.\r\n\r\nThis explanation might seem lengthy and complicated, but the case is not common, but also can happen so it needs to be mentioned. The abort operation can result in that unique naming, so don’t abort if you don’t really need to. Just wait for the program to finish its job.\r\n\r\n- Undo: you can undo only one-step backward (the immediate last change). The number of filenames that has been changed is re-counted at each change, or when the program starts.
